<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes"><a href = vnd.unilang:usage.html>Usage</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:note.html>notes</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>In</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scientific.html>scientific</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:discourse.html>discourse</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> “unproven conjecture” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> discouraged (<a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:hypothesis.html>hypothesis</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:conjecture.html>conjecture</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:preferred.html>preferred</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:due.html>due</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> unintentional <a href = vnd.unilang:ambiguity.html>ambiguity</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:intentional.html>intentional</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:equivocation.html>equivocation</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sense.html>sense</a> “well-developed <a href = vnd.unilang:statement.html>statement</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> structure”.

<h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:theory.html>theory</a></b>
